Know Yourself
It seems there are many people meeting the teacher for the first time today, so let's see a show of hands. Originally, you were supposed to have an engagement ceremony before the Holy Wine Ceremony today. Since you are sitting with your spouses, let's substitute the engagement ceremony by holding each other's hands tightly. Then we can start the Holy Wine Ceremony.
How many of the people to be blessed are Korean? Then, in which language should we begin? Should the teacher speak in Japanese and have it interpreted into English? Interpretation is always an issue at times like this. How will we solve this problem in the future? This is also a global issue.
Today, since there are many Japanese members gathered here, the teacher will speak in Japanese and Oyamada will interpret into English. (Applause) Then, won't the Korean members have difficulty? We will have it interpreted for the Korean members to read on the screen.
The Holy Wine Ceremony is the Blood Lineage Conversion Ceremony
As taught before, it is customary to have an engagement ceremony followed by a wedding ceremony. In the Garden of Eden, Adam and Eve fell before reaching the time of engagement and marriage. To indemnify and restore this, you must complete the engagement ceremony and then convert the blood lineage. This blood lineage conversion ceremony is precisely the Holy Wine Ceremony.
From the perspective of the Unification Church's principles, every human must pass through the process of indemnity and return to the original state to restore the blood lineage. Therefore, you must pass through the engagement and wedding ceremonies that Adam and Eve could not complete as the final point of settlement. This is the current Holy Wine Ceremony, the Blood Lineage Conversion Ceremony.
What is the root of the Fall?
The ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, fell during the engagement period. Looking at the history of the world, it is evident in every aspect that it is not a good history. Seeing this, we cannot deny that humanity has fallen. Therefore, the teacher is teaching you clearly that the ancestors of humanity have fallen.
Then, what exactly is the Fall? And the Bible says Adam and Eve fell by eating the fruit of the tree of knowledge of good and evil. What is that fruit? The symbolic fruit of the tree of knowledge of good and evil has never been interpreted by anyone until now. But the teacher has come and revealed its contents concretely for the first time. Ultimately, what was the result of the Fall? The ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, were expelled from the Garden of Eden by God.
Therefore, what is questionable in your standards? Did Adam and Eve have children in the Garden of Eden before being expelled, or did they have children after being expelled? If this is not clarified, the root of fallen humanity will not be clear. Think about it. The answer is simple.
9 
Adam and Eve had children after being expelled, meaning they lived a married life. 
Then, did God, who expelled Adam and Eve, interfere with their married life, or did they live a married life from a position that God did not favor? In conclusion, Adam and Eve lived a married life without interference from God and from a position that God did not favor. The fallen Adam and Eve were beyond God's interference.
Then, centered on whom and what did they live a married life? Ultimately, it cannot be denied that they started their married life centered on Satan. Because they became a couple centered on Satan, they inherited Satan's love, Satan's life, and Satan's blood lineage.
What is the root of the Fall? It is the violation of heavenly law through love centered on Satan. They inherited Satan's life and blood lineage through Satan's love and passed it on to their descendants. Since humanity has fallen under Satan's blood lineage, restoring and saving it is not a simple matter.
If Adam and Eve had not fallen, what would have happened? You must know this clearly. In the created world, everything is made in pairs, right? Male and female, man and woman, plus and minus. Since the created world is made this way, it is known that humans must become one as man and woman when they mature.
If God had blessed the matured Adam and Eve, true couples inheriting true love, true life, and true blood lineage centered on God would have emerged and expanded into true families, true tribes, true nations, and a true world. However, humanity lost the True Parents due to the Fall. As a result, false parents emerged, and hell was created. Erasing the history of false parents and reinstating the history of True Parents is God's providence.
10   
Humanity standing at the boundary between heaven and hell due to the Fall
God intended to open the way to heaven through the True Parents, but as a result, false parents emerged, opening the way to hell, and the way to heaven was not opened. Humanity, standing at the boundary between heaven and hell, is the self. You must know this clearly.
Every human has a conscience and a body. Originally, centered on true love, the conscience and body were to automatically resonate and become one. They were to automatically resonate centered on true love. However, as a result of trying to become one centered on false love, the conscience and body ended up in a position where they repel each other. This is the current position of each person and the world.
From your perspective, the left side is connected to hell. Then, what is connected to the right side? Heaven. And what is related to the left side is the body, and what is related to the right side is the conscience. No one has known that the fight between these two has continued centered on oneself throughout history. But with the emergence of the Unification Church, this has become clear.
As a result of the Fall, individuals have split into two, centered on themselves, left and right. There is no center. Therefore, humanity has wandered back and forth. They do not know the direction to go. This is the global phenomenon at the end times. There are many leaders in the world, but no one knows where to go in the future. They do not know whether to go left or right, forward or backward. Therefore, there is no way to resolve the world into the direction of the ideal world of creation centered on the world's leaders.
Satan denies God, and what does God do to Satan? Does He welcome him? He denies him. In the midst of both sides denying each other, we do not know how to proceed. Therefore, there has been a fight between Cain and Abel, good and evil, throughout history.
11 
Who struck first among them? Throughout history, the larger, higher position has always struck first. Centered on the providence of restoration, the firstborn in the position of the larger side is on Satan's side, and the second-born is on God's side.
Thus, we cannot help but distinguish between Satan's side and God's side. The fight between Abel, representing God's side, and Cain, representing Satan's side, began in the family, as seen in the Bible's story of Cain and Abel. As a result, Satan stands in front, followed by Adam, then Eve, then the firstborn Cain, and finally the second-born Abel.
Therefore, when God tried to find the representative of the world of conscience in Adam's family, He took the lowest position. Since Satan took the head, God could not help but take the tail. Thus, God tried to restore Cain through Abel, who was in the position of the younger brother. He intended to place the younger brother in the position of the elder brother and the elder brother in the position of the younger brother. It is 180 degrees opposite. This fight has extended throughout human history.
God's strategy of receiving blows and reclaiming history
The body represents politics. Cain, standing on Satan's side, represents politics wielding power with the right of the firstborn, and Abel, on the opposite side, represents religion standing on God's side. Knowing that if religion is established within the earthly Satanic realm, the Satanic realm will be entirely destroyed, Satan fundamentally tries to block the emergence of religion. Therefore, rulers have persecuted religious realms with Satan's power, and many righteous people have shed blood.
In this way, the right side, the Abel realm, must go to the left side, the Cain realm, and digest everything from the individual to the family, tribe, people, nation, world, and finally hell. Without denying everything about oneself, one cannot find the way to heaven. One must take the method of naturally subjugating Satan by going 180 degrees to the opposite side, not by striking and subjugating.
God Himself does not have the concept of an enemy. There is no concept of fighting with God. Otherwise, He would be the same as Satan. Therefore, God goes to Satan's realm, receives blows, and reclaims through indemnity, restoring the individual, family, tribe, people, nation, and connecting to the world. There is a separate strategy for finding this path. God's strategy is not to strike and reclaim but to receive blows and demand compensation. This is how it has developed to the world level. Do you understand?
By doing so, the right-wing centered on the religious realm and the left-wing centered on the political realm become one. And the traditional history of God's side continues as it has flowed from Adam and Eve through Abel. The providence of restoration must pass through the main course.
Then, where is such a main religion? The history of Judaism did not develop on its own. It wandered like a gypsy. Abraham did, too, didn't he? Abraham received the word from God to leave his homeland and go to Satan's homeland. Jacob did the same, didn't he? After receiving the blessing from his father, he went to Egypt. He went to Satan's homeland. Christianity is the same. It entered based on the opposing Roman Empire.
Therefore, Satan knows well that God will eliminate the Satanic realm in the future. So Satan fought comprehensively. In the midst of this, many people have shed blood throughout history. You must know that you must expand the victorious realm of the religious realm, which has inherited such a tradition, to connect the tribe, people, nation, world, and cosmos.
In this way, what is the relationship between Judaism, Christianity, and the Unification Church? They are in the relationship of formation, growth, and completion. Also, what is the mission of the teacher? It is to restore the national standard lost by Jesus' death and develop it to the world level to naturally subjugate the Satanic realm. Jesus left the word of the Second Coming because he could not complete his mission on earth. And Jesus' death left the right-wing, left-wing, and Barabbas realms at the national standard.
Therefore, the Second Coming must unify the right-wing, left-wing, and Barabbas realms. The Second Coming must resolve the world-level cross centered on Jesus' death, organizing the left, right, and the Barabbas realm in front. Since all human history has passed through Jesus' death, the Second Coming must quickly resolve this. Do you understand?
Restoring Eve and Cain and Abel on a global standard
In the Garden of Eden, the woman fell first, right? That woman was expelled by God, got married, and bore the firstborn and the second-born. These three were ultimately lost from God's side. They should have given birth to completed children before the completed Adam, but they abandoned the victorious realm of the ideal Adam and went to Satan. They abandoned the foundation that should have been one with God and went away. Ultimately, they went to Satan and became Satan's, and their children also became Satan's.
This is the result of standing in a position that cannot be allowed in the principle of creation. The strategy to reverse this result is what God has been moving history through the religious realm.
Without restoring such Eve and Cain and Abel from Satan, God cannot establish the family He originally intended. Without a family, there is no tribe, people, nation, or world. Therefore, the family must be restored. Without restoring Satan's Eve and Cain and Abel, the family problem in the Satanic world cannot be fundamentally solved, and the family cannot be unified with God's side.
Therefore, contrary to the Satanic Eve and Cain and Abel forming a global nation, God's Eve and Cain and Abel must be globally united and made one. Do you understand?
Thus, in the providence, at the end of human history, the victorious realm of Cain and Abel is organized centered on Eve. It must be organized centered on God to establish the victorious standard that digests the Satanic side. Then, centered on the completed Adam, the foundation of family, tribe, people, and nation is organized. By moving the left-wing and right-wing centered on Adam to God's side, the Satanic world disappears. This should have been accomplished right after World War II.
Isn't the United Kingdom an island nation? An island nation symbolizes a woman. Centered on the United Kingdom, Abel and the archangel are established, with Abel being the United States, born from the United Kingdom. France was once the enemy of the United Kingdom, so it is the archangel. God's Eve, God's Abel, and God's archangel become one.
Conversely, the Satanic Eve established is Japan, Japan. Japan is also an island nation, right? An island in the East. And Germany is the Satanic Abel nation, and the Satanic archangel nation is Italy. Italy goes back and forth, right? France also goes back and forth. So they are archangel nations.
Thus, the world was divided into two camps and fought in World War II. And with the victory of the Allied Forces, a world centered on God was historically established. The religious realm unified the world at that time. Do you understand so far?
Without clearly understanding history, you cannot clearly recognize the providence. Since the Satanic Eve nation, Abel, and archangel nations returned to God's side, it is the end times. The end times, the end times. However, the unified blood lineage of Cain and Abel is not inherited from God. Since it is inherited from Satan, the false parents, it must all be indemnified and returned to God. Eve and Cain and Abel must inherit the new seed of life centered on true love after clearing all Satanic things to become God's children. The substantial being that inherits this new seed of life is the Second Coming, the Savior, and the True Parents.

All beings are made as subject and object because of true love
In the environment, there must be a subject and an object. The providence of salvation is the providence of restoration, and the providence of restoration is the providence of re-creation. What is that? When God created, He made the environment, and within it, there were subjects and objects. In the world of molecules, there are positive ions and negative ions, and in the world of electricity, there are positive and negative charges. Why are they relatively made like that? Although the level is low, it is to act centered on love.

Even in plants, there are pistils and stamens, right? Why are they like that? It is to act centered on love and reproduce. Anything that does not perpetuate centered on love cannot maintain its historical existence. Everything is made that way.

In the animal world, there are males and females, right? Even if you rummage through the grass right now, no matter how small the insect, they are all made as males and females. They are made like that, right? It is now announced that even bacteria have male and female.

And why are men and women made like that? Is it women and men, or men and women? Does it matter which side? It doesn't matter, right? Being made as a connected body to have a counterpart relationship is for love. Anything, when centered on love, receives applause and harmony from the surroundings. If Adam and Eve and God achieve the unity of love, heaven and earth will harmonize together, right? Even if not directly connected, through the resonance of the felt wavelength, heaven and earth will harmonize. Therefore, in the realm of creation, there must be a subject and an object.

Now, let me ask you one thing. Everyone! Is evolution first, or is the concept of male and female first? Which one is first? This is a serious problem. To overthrow communism, we must clearly understand the logic that can overcome evolution. Did the amoeba exist before the phenomenal world, or after? How is it connected from the amoeba to humans?

The concept that the substance develops through love is ignored, and the foolish logic that humans evolved from amoebas is nowhere in the world. How can you explain the birth of men and women, the emergence of males and females? Is the concept of love first, or is the birth of men and women first? Which one is it? This is a serious problem. Which one is it? The conclusion is that the concept of love is first.

A public person must be entirely public. But in love, there is freedom, I mean, only in love. Because they are together, they can love even while starving and love even while dying. If a couple starves to death together, claiming 'Our couple is the best,' they can become the best. Because they have no strength, they can only hold on and die, right? So you must love. (Laughter) It's true. 

In love, there is freedom. It's all about how you love. Is there anything better than that? Is there any privilege better than that? There is no freedom like that. The kingship of freedom is there. Kingship is there. Those who live connected to parents and the world centered on such a loving couple become the owners of the heavenly kingdom. They become a royal family with kingship. 

Looking at it this way, will the teacher go to hell or heaven? "You will go to heaven." I don't even think about going to heaven. (Laughter) The issue is whether I fulfilled my mission or not. Heaven is secondary. If I go, I go; if I don't, I don't. If I can't go, I can take those who like me and live together, right? If the teacher shows them spiritually, how well will they serve and do? Heaven is not elsewhere. It's the same. So where is there greater liberation than that? Now, has the time come for the teacher to be liberated, or not? "It has come." Then what should you do when you go home? 

If you want to serve the teacher, you must serve the nation, and to serve the nation, you must have a tribe. Only then can you hold a banquet or serve anywhere. Will you serve alone? That's why you must become a tribal messiah. Then you naturally become the center of the nation. 

If you serve the teacher, will you serve alone, or will you serve with your couple? "No!" Then what is it? You must gather at least a tribe, create a subject-object... That's the principle of creation. You must create a subject-object to serve. Shouldn't the nation unite to serve? Isn't that right? That's why missionaries were sent. So you must go alone and give birth to and raise a tribe. 

You must give birth to the entire world population again
What is evangelism? It means to give birth and raise. The person who evangelizes becomes the father of faith. Evangelism means giving birth to dead people again. Now you must give birth to the entire world population again. Will that be easy or difficult? That's why you are doing something that ordinary people find difficult. People who live to eat... if they go without food for a week... well, most will die in ten days. But we survive even after fasting for 40 days. Many people fast for 40 days, right? There is something that allows us to survive. But Western people pant even if they miss just one meal. 

How pitiful are people who live hanging on one meal? Unification Church members fast for a week, so going without food for a day or three is normal. No matter how unfortunate and unlucky, can't you eat one meal in three days? (Laughter) You can live like that. So in God's eyes, who is loyal? A person who eats three meals a day or someone who eats one less meal?
It's high. The more you skip two meals, the higher it is. That's how it is. If someone doesn't go even a single point from zero in a week, they are the first place. It's zero, zero. That's the truth.

From that perspective, since the teacher is the Messiah, he must go to prison the most. "It's a call from Mother." Mom! "Father! You said you were in the middle of a speech, didn't you?" The speech is over now. I'm talking extra now. "Oh, really?" Did you hear what prayer was said? Mother needs to know. "I didn't hear it." If you didn't hear it, you have to record everything again and study it. Call and copy it…. "Yes! All the members who are at the event today have gone out." 'Members' is 'old style.' When God sees it, it becomes old style. So, it has to be new style.

What time is it now? "It's 7 o'clock." It's 6 o'clock here, so it's an hour difference! Well, it's just an hour difference…. Do well today! Since you listened to Dad's words energetically today, knowing what position Mother stands in, you must reign energetically like a queen. Do you understand?

I'm suffering like this to pave the way for Mother. So, even if it's just one pancake, you have to make it sincerely. "Where are you going after paving the way for Mother?" (Laughter) Look, everyone is laughing! "Why are you making it public when it's just between us?" It's time for that. Now everything must be revealed! The secrets of the Heavenly Kingdom and the secrets on earth are all being revealed. Even Satan is being revealed. You have to reveal yourself to settle everything.

Where in the world is there no Unification Church now? They hold three-day events, indemnity stick events…. Because they don't want to talk about it, Satan says, "Hey, you fools! You useless kids!" and hits them. You have to repent after being hit to come to your senses! Now everything has been revealed.

Mom! "Yes!" Today, it's the day the trainees here are having a commemorative ceremony, so maybe a gift…. Did you prepare something there too? "Yes!" Give all the tables here, and exchange what's here with what's over there! "Yes!" (Laughter) Now that it's exchanged, consider this as given by Mother and that side as given by Father and distribute it! Do it like that. "Yes, thank you." Take care. Mom, finish quickly and come back soon. I want to see you soon. (Applause)

From now on, we will celebrate these congratulatory days together with the parents. It's like showing everything at a wedding. You have to know that we are the only ones doing this globally. Even America can't do it. Only we can do it. "Father, see you later!" Yes. Thank you. Mother's voice is very kind and familiar, but someone next to her is holding and talking. "Father, be happy today!" Yes, thank you. Mother, succeed today. "Yes!" I'll pray for you. Today is a day that Heaven and Earth rejoice. (Ends phone call with Mother.)

The center that can make a family run is a woman. "If you just set up a set where the parents are, the plate…. It's really simple." The substantial God is like that. This is developed because of us. Here, the teacher is using everything at the cutting edge. Our audio system or video system in America is the best in the world. The television center is also the best broadcasting in the world. Everything is prepared like that. The teacher will do it for your countries too. So, if you call the president and the ministers…. Now it's your responsibility. If you can't take responsibility, don't come. We won't call you. That's why women are mobilized. That's the principle.

How can a family run? The man is not the center. It's not the sons and daughters; the woman is the center. By forming a family on this earth and running it, the family starts from now in the spirit world. First, on this earth…. The place where the ideal family enters is the spirit world. Is that so? The place where plus and minus, subject and object become one and enter is the spirit world. This is re-creation. Do you understand? "Yes." Who is the center? In running, who is the center? "It's the woman." (The subsequent words could not be recorded due to poor recording condition.) *
